[1mNAME[0m[m
       find - search for files in a directory hierarchy[m
[m
[1mSYNOPSIS[0m[m
       [1mfind  [22m[-H]  [-L] [-P] [-D debugopts] [-Olevel] [starting-point...] [ex‐[m
       pression][m
[m
[1mDESCRIPTION[0m[m
       This manual page documents the GNU version of [1mfind[22m.  GNU [1mfind  [22msearches[m
       the  directory  tree  rooted at each given starting-point by evaluating[m
       the given expression from left to right,  according  to  the  rules  of[m
       precedence  (see  section  OPERATORS),  until the outcome is known (the[m
       left hand side is false for [4mand[24m operations,  true  for  [4mor[24m),  at  which[m
       point  [1mfind  [22mmoves  on  to the next file name.  If no starting-point is[m
       specified, `.' is assumed.[m
[m
       If you are using [1mfind [22min an environment  where  security  is  important[m
       (for  example  if  you  are  using  it  to  search directories that are[m
       writable by other users), you should read the `Security Considerations'[m
       chapter of the findutils documentation, which is called  [1mFinding  Files[0m[m
       and  comes  with findutils.  That document also includes a lot more de‐[m

[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       tail and discussion than this manual page, so you may find  it  a  more[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 2 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       useful source of information.[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 3 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K

[4mFIND[24m(1)                     General Commands Manual                    [4mFIND[24m(1)[m
[m
[1mNAME[0m[m
       find - search for files in a directory hierarchy[m
[m
[1mSYNOPSIS[0m[m
       [1mfind  [22m[-H]  [-L] [-P] [-D debugopts] [-Olevel] [starting-point...] [ex‐[m
       pression][m
[m
[1mDESCRIPTION[0m[m
       This manual page documents the GNU version of [1mfind[22m.  GNU [1mfind  [22msearches[m
       the  directory  tree  rooted at each given starting-point by evaluating[m
       the given expression from left to right,  according  to  the  rules  of[m
       precedence  (see  section  OPERATORS),  until the outcome is known (the[m
       left hand side is false for [4mand[24m operations,  true  for  [4mor[24m),  at  which[m
       point  [1mfind  [22mmoves  on  to the next file name.  If no starting-point is[m
       specified, `.' is assumed.[m
[m
       If you are using [1mfind [22min an environment  where  security  is  important[m
       (for  example  if  you  are  using  it  to  search directories that are[m
       writable by other users), you should read the `Security Considerations'[m
       chapter of the findutils documentation, which is called  [1mFinding  Files[0m[m
       and  comes  with findutils.  That document also includes a lot more de‐[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 1 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       tail and discussion than this manual page, so you may find  it  a  more[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 2 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       useful source of information.[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 3 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K

[4mFIND[24m(1)                     General Commands Manual                    [4mFIND[24m(1)[m
[m
[1mNAME[0m[m
       find - search for files in a directory hierarchy[m
[m
[1mSYNOPSIS[0m[m
       [1mfind  [22m[-H]  [-L] [-P] [-D debugopts] [-Olevel] [starting-point...] [ex‐[m
       pression][m
[m
[1mDESCRIPTION[0m[m
       This manual page documents the GNU version of [1mfind[22m.  GNU [1mfind  [22msearches[m
       the  directory  tree  rooted at each given starting-point by evaluating[m
       the given expression from left to right,  according  to  the  rules  of[m
       precedence  (see  section  OPERATORS),  until the outcome is known (the[m
       left hand side is false for [4mand[24m operations,  true  for  [4mor[24m),  at  which[m
       point  [1mfind  [22mmoves  on  to the next file name.  If no starting-point is[m
       specified, `.' is assumed.[m
[m
       If you are using [1mfind [22min an environment  where  security  is  important[m
       (for  example  if  you  are  using  it  to  search directories that are[m
       writable by other users), you should read the `Security Considerations'[m
       chapter of the findutils documentation, which is called  [1mFinding  Files[0m[m
       and  comes  with findutils.  That document also includes a lot more de‐[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 1 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       tail and discussion than this manual page, so you may find  it  a  more[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 2 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       useful source of information.[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 3 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 4 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K[1mOPTIONS[0m[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 5 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       The  [1m-H[22m,  [1m-L  [22mand  [1m-P  [22moptions control the treatment of symbolic links.[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 6 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       Command-line arguments following these are taken to be names  of  files[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 7 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       or  directories  to  be  examined, up to the first argument that begins[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 8 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       with `-', or the argument `(' or `!'.  That argument and any  following[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 9 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       arguments  are  taken  to  be  the  expression describing what is to be[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 10 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       searched for.  If no paths are given, the current  directory  is  used.[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 11 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       If  no  expression  is  given,  the  expression [1m-print [22mis used (but you[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 12 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       should probably consider using [1m-print0 [22minstead, anyway).[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 13 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 14 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       This manual page talks about  `options'  within  the  expression  list.[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 15 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       These  options  control the behaviour of [1mfind [22mbut are specified immedi‐[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 16 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       ately after the last path name.  The five `real' options [1m-H[22m, [1m-L[22m, [1m-P[22m, [1m-D[0m[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 17 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       and [1m-O [22mmust appear before the first path name, if  at  all.   A  double[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 18 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       dash  [1m-- [22mcould theoretically be used to signal that any remaining argu‐[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 19 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       ments are not options, but this does not really work  due  to  the  way[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 20 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       [1mfind  [22mdetermines  the end of the following path arguments: it does that[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 21 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       by reading until an expression argument comes (which also starts with a[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 22 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       `-').  Now, if a path argument would start with a `-', then [1mfind  [22mwould[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 23 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       treat  it  as  expression  argument  instead.  Thus, to ensure that all[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 24 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       start points are taken as such, and especially to prevent that wildcard[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 25 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       patterns expanded by the calling shell are not  mistakenly  treated  as[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 26 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       expression  arguments, it is generally safer to prefix wildcards or du‐[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 27 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       bious path names with either `./' or to use absolute path names  start‐[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 28 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       ing  with '/'.  Alternatively, it is generally safe though non-portable[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 29 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       to use the GNU option [1m-files0-from [22mto pass arbitrary starting points to[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 30 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       [1mfind[22m.[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 31 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 32 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       -P     Never follow symbolic links.  This  is  the  default  behaviour.[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 33 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K              When  [1mfind  [22mexamines  or prints information about files, and the[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 34 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K              file is a symbolic link, the information  used  shall  be  taken[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 35 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K              from the properties of the symbolic link itself.[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 36 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 37 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       -L     Follow symbolic links.  When [1mfind [22mexamines or prints information[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 38 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K

[4mFIND[24m(1)                     General Commands Manual                    [4mFIND[24m(1)[m
[m
[1mNAME[0m[m
       find - search for files in a directory hierarchy[m
[m
[1mSYNOPSIS[0m[m
       [1mfind  [22m[-H]  [-L] [-P] [-D debugopts] [-Olevel] [starting-point...] [ex‐[m
       pression][m
[m
[1mDESCRIPTION[0m[m
       This manual page documents the GNU version of [1mfind[22m.  GNU [1mfind  [22msearches[m
       the  directory  tree  rooted at each given starting-point by evaluating[m
       the given expression from left to right,  according  to  the  rules  of[m
       precedence  (see  section  OPERATORS),  until the outcome is known (the[m
       left hand side is false for [4mand[24m operations,  true  for  [4mor[24m),  at  which[m
       point  [1mfind  [22mmoves  on  to the next file name.  If no starting-point is[m
       specified, `.' is assumed.[m
[m
       If you are using [1mfind [22min an environment  where  security  is  important[m
       (for  example  if  you  are  using  it  to  search directories that are[m
       writable by other users), you should read the `Security Considerations'[m
       chapter of the findutils documentation, which is called  [1mFinding  Files[0m[m
       and  comes  with findutils.  That document also includes a lot more de‐[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 1 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       tail and discussion than this manual page, so you may find  it  a  more[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 2 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       useful source of information.[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 3 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 4 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K[1mOPTIONS[0m[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 5 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       The  [1m-H[22m,  [1m-L  [22mand  [1m-P  [22moptions control the treatment of symbolic links.[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 6 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       Command-line arguments following these are taken to be names  of  files[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 7 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       or  directories  to  be  examined, up to the first argument that begins[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 8 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       with `-', or the argument `(' or `!'.  That argument and any  following[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 9 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       arguments  are  taken  to  be  the  expression describing what is to be[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 10 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       searched for.  If no paths are given, the current  directory  is  used.[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 11 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       If  no  expression  is  given,  the  expression [1m-print [22mis used (but you[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 12 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       should probably consider using [1m-print0 [22minstead, anyway).[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 13 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB

[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       This manual page talks about  `options'  within  the  expression  list.[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 15 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K

[7m Manual page find(1) line 16 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB

[4mFIND[24m(1)                     General Commands Manual                    [4mFIND[24m(1)[m
[m
[1mNAME[0m[m
       find - search for files in a directory hierarchy[m
[m
[1mSYNOPSIS[0m[m
       [1mfind  [22m[-H]  [-L] [-P] [-D debugopts] [-Olevel] [starting-point...] [ex‐[m
       pression][m
[m
[1mDESCRIPTION[0m[m
       This manual page documents the GNU version of [1mfind[22m.  GNU [1mfind  [22msearches[m
       the  directory  tree  rooted at each given starting-point by evaluating[m
       the given expression from left to right,  according  to  the  rules  of[m
       precedence  (see  section  OPERATORS),  until the outcome is known (the[m
       left hand side is false for [4mand[24m operations,  true  for  [4mor[24m),  at  which[m
       point  [1mfind  [22mmoves  on  to the next file name.  If no starting-point is[m
       specified, `.' is assumed.[m
[m
       If you are using [1mfind [22min an environment  where  security  is  important[m
       (for  example  if  you  are  using  it  to  search directories that are[m
       writable by other users), you should read the `Security Considerations'[m
       chapter of the findutils documentation, which is called  [1mFinding  Files[0m[m
       and  comes  with findutils.  That document also includes a lot more de‐[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 1 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       tail and discussion than this manual page, so you may find  it  a  more[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 2 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       useful source of information.[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 3 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 4 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KAA

[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       The  [1m-H[22m,  [1m-L  [22mand  [1m-P  [22moptions control the treatment of symbolic links.[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 6 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       Command-line arguments following these are taken to be names  of  files[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 7 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       or  directories  to  be  examined, up to the first argument that begins[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 8 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       with `-', or the argument `(' or `!'.  That argument and any  following[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 9 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       arguments  are  taken  to  be  the  expression describing what is to be[m
[7m Manual page find(1) line 10 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K

[1mNAME[0m[m
       mv - move (rename) files[m
[m
[1mSYNOPSIS[0m[m
       [1mmv [22m[[4mOPTION[24m]... [[4m-T[24m] [4mSOURCE[24m [4mDEST[0m[m
       [1mmv [22m[[4mOPTION[24m]... [4mSOURCE[24m... [4mDIRECTORY[0m[m
       [1mmv [22m[[4mOPTION[24m]... [4m-t[24m [4mDIRECTORY[24m [4mSOURCE[24m...[m
[m
[1mDESCRIPTION[0m[m
       Rename SOURCE to DEST, or move SOURCE(s) to DIRECTORY.[m
[m
       Mandatory  arguments  to  long  options are mandatory for short options[m
       too.[m
[m
       [1m--backup[22m[=[4mCONTROL[24m][m
              make a backup of each existing destination file[m
[m
       [1m-b     [22mlike [1m--backup [22mbut does not accept an argument[m
[m
       [1m--debug[0m[m
              explain how a file is copied.  Implies [1m-v[0m[m
